```html
<script>
   (function () {
    const section = document.currentScript.closest('.category-grid-template--27935319916710__category_grid_tiRJL3') || document;
    const layouts = section.querySelectorAll('.category-layout-template--27935319916710__category_grid_tiRJL3');
    if (!layouts.length) return;

    let index = 0;
    const intervalTime = 4000;
    let intervalId;

    // Make layouts focusable for keyboard navigation
    layouts.forEach((layout) => {
      layout.setAttribute('tabindex', '0'); // allows layout to receive focus
    });

    // Show a specific layout
    const showLayout = (i) => {
      layouts.forEach((el, j) => el.classList.toggle('is-active', j === i));
      index = i;
    };

    // Start automatic rotation
    const startRotation = () => {
      intervalId = setInterval(() => {
        const nextIndex = (index + 1) % layouts.length;
        showLayout(nextIndex);
      }, intervalTime);
    };

    // Stop rotation
    const stopRotation = () => {
      clearInterval(intervalId);
    };

   
    showLayout(0);
    startRotation();

    // Handle focus on entire layouts
    layouts.forEach((layout, i) => {
      layout.addEventListener('focus', () => {
        showLayout(i);   
        stopRotation();   
      });

      layout.addEventListener('blur', () => {
        startRotation();  // resume rotation when focus leaves
      });

      // Optional: allow Enter or Space to click first link inside layout
      layout.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
        if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
          e.preventDefault();
          const firstLink = layout.querySelector('a');
          if (firstLink) firstLink.click();
        }
      });
    });

   
    section.querySelectorAll('.category-layout-template--27935319916710__category_grid_tiRJL3 a').forEach((link) => {
      link.addEventListener('focus', () => stopRotation());
      link.addEventListener('blur', () => startRotation());
    });
  })();
</script>


</div>
```

```html
      <span class="visually-hidden">&nbsp;per&nbsp;</span>
      <span>
      </span>
    </span>
  </small>
</div>

        </div>

        
        
        
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</product-card>

                      
                    
                  </div>
                  
                </div>
              
            </div>
          <span class="swiper-notification" aria-live="assertive" aria-atomic="true"></span></div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>



<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  const section = document.querySelector('#cs-template--27935319916710__trending_collection_BcHBQD');
  if (!section) return;

  const names = section.querySelectorAll('.cs-name');
  const cards = section.querySelectorAll('.rummy-card');

  const states = [
    { x: 0, r: 0, s: 1, z: 3 },
    { x: -20, r: -6, s: 0.96, z: 2 },
    { x: 20, r: 6, s: 0.94, z: 1 },
  ];

  function updateRummy(index) {
    cards.forEach((card, i) => {
      const pos = states[(i - index + states.length) % states.length];
      card.style.transform = `translateX(${pos.x}px) rotate(${pos.r}deg) scale(${pos.s})`;
      card.style.zIndex = pos.z;
      card.classList.toggle('back', pos.z !== 3);
    });
  }

  whenSwiperReady(() => {

    const swiper = new Swiper('.cs-swiper-template--27935319916710__trending_collection_BcHBQD', {
      effect: 'fade',
      speed: 800,
      allowTouchMove: false,
      init: false,
    });

    let slidesCount = 0;
    let lastIndex = 0;

    swiper.on('init', () => {

      slidesCount = swiper.slides.length;

      /* SECTION HEIGHT FOR STICKY EFFECT (ALL DEVICES) */
      
      if (window.innerWidth > 768) {
        section.style.height = `${slidesCount * 100}vh`; // desktop sticky scroll
      } else {
        section.style.height = 'auto'; // mobile normal scroll
      }

      swiper.slideTo(0, 0);
      updateRummy(0);

      names.forEach((n) => n.classList.remove('active'));
      if (names[0]) names[0].classList.add('active');
    });

    swiper.on('slideChange', () => {
      const i = swiper.activeIndex;

      names.forEach((n) => n.classList.remove('active'));
      if (names[i]) names[i].classList.add('active');

      updateRummy(i);
    });

    swiper.init();

    /* DESKTOP → SCROLL CONTROL */
    if (window.innerWidth > 768) {
      window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {

        const rect = section.getBoundingClientRect();
        const maxScroll = (slidesCount - 1) * window.innerHeight;

        if (rect.top <= 0 && Math.abs(rect.top) <= maxScroll) {

          const progress = Math.abs(rect.top) / maxScroll;
          const index = Math.round(progress * (slidesCount - 1));

          if (index !== lastIndex) {
            swiper.slideTo(index);
            lastIndex = index;
          }
        }

      });
    }

    /* MOBILE → CLICK CONTROL */
    if (window.innerWidth <= 768) {

      names.forEach((name, i) => {

        name.addEventListener('click', () => {

          swiper.slideTo(i);

          names.forEach((n) => n.classList.remove('active'));
          name.classList.add('active');

          updateRummy(i);

        });

      });

    }

  });

});
</script>


</div>
```

```html
<script>
  var imageRoot = document.querySelector('.image-video-hero-template--27935319916710__scroll_zoom_video_image_cXGUUp');
  var imageVideo = imageRoot.querySelector('video');
  if (imageVideo) {
    imageVideo.querySelector('img').setAttribute('alt', 'Video scroll image');
  }
</script>

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {

  const section = document.querySelector('.section-template--27935319916710__scroll_zoom_video_image_cXGUUp');
  if (!section) return;

  const media = section.querySelector('.brand_media img, .brand_media video, .brand_media svg');
  const leftText = section.querySelector('.left_text');
  const rightText = section.querySelector('.right_text');

  const startScale = window.innerWidth < 1024 ? 0.35 : 0.13;
  const endScale = 1;

  function animate() {

    if (window.innerWidth < 768) return;

    const rect = section.getBoundingClientRect();
    const windowHeight = window.innerHeight;

    const totalScroll = section.offsetHeight - windowHeight;
    const scrolled = Math.min(Math.max(-rect.top, 0), totalScroll);

    let overallProgress = scrolled / totalScroll;
    overallProgress = Math.min(Math.max(overallProgress, 0), 1);

    /* -------------------------
       SPLIT INTO 2 PHASES
    --------------------------*/

    const zoomEndPoint = 0.7; // zoom finishes at 70%

    let zoomProgress;

    if (overallProgress <= zoomEndPoint) {
      zoomProgress = overallProgress / zoomEndPoint;
    } else {
      zoomProgress = 1; // Hold full zoom
    }

    const eased = Math.pow(zoomProgress, 0.85);

    /* ZOOM */
    const scale = startScale + (endScale - startScale) * eased;
    media.style.transform = `scale(${scale})`;

    /* TEXT MOVE */
    const maxShift = section.offsetWidth * 0.08;
    const shift = maxShift * eased;

    leftText.style.transform = `translate(-${shift}px, -50%)`;
    rightText.style.transform = `translate(${shift}px, -50%)`;
  }

  window.addEventListener('scroll', animate, { passive: true });
  window.addEventListener('resize', animate);
  animate();

});
</script>




</div>
```

```html
<script>
  
(function () {
  const wrapper = document.getElementById('ba-template--27935319916710__before_after_QniKY7');
  if (!wrapper) return;

  const afterImg = wrapper.querySelector('.ba-after');
  const divider = wrapper.querySelector('.ba-divider');

  let dragging = false;

  function move(x) {
    const rect = wrapper.getBoundingClientRect();
    let pos = x - rect.left;

    pos = Math.max(0, Math.min(pos, rect.width));

    const percent = (pos / rect.width) * 100;

   afterImg.style.clipPath = `inset(0 0 0 ${percent}%)`;
    divider.style.left = percent + '%';
  }

  divider.addEventListener('mousedown', () => dragging = true);
  divider.addEventListener('touchstart', () => dragging = true);

  window.addEventListener('mouseup', () => dragging = false);
  window.addEventListener('touchend', () => dragging = false);

  window.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => dragging && move(e.clientX));
  window.addEventListener('touchmove', (e) => dragging && move(e.touches[0].clientX));

  /* INITIAL POSITION FIX */
  move(wrapper.getBoundingClientRect().left + wrapper.offsetWidth / 2);

})();

</script>

</div>


</div>
```

```html
                    <h3 class="pdp_title">Pure Argan Milk Intensive Hydrating Treatment</h3>
                  

                
            
              
                  <div class="f_product_price_container">
                    <p class="pdp_price">$4.00</p>
                    <del class="pdp_c_price"></del>
                  </div>

                
            
              
                  <div class="product_description">
                    <p>Pure Argan Milk Intensive Hydrating Treatment harnesses the nourishing power of argan oil to deliver deep moisture and restore skin's natural radiance. This lightweight yet potent formula penetrates quickly, infusing dehydrated skin with essential fatty acids and antioxidants. Ideal for all skin types, particularly those prone to dryness or sensitivity, this treatment strengthens the skin barrier while promoting a smoother, more luminous complexion. Apply to clean skin as a targeted treatment or layer beneath your moisturizer for enhanced hydration benefits.</p>
```

```html
  <script>
    whenSwiperReady(() => {
  const customDots = document.querySelectorAll('.custom_dots--template--27935319916710__products_hotspot_9BRLnf');

  const cards_swiper = new Swiper('.pdp_cards_slider--template--27935319916710__products_hotspot_9BRLnf', {
    effect: 'cards',
    grabCursor: true,
    centeredSlides: true,
    initialSlide: 1,
    cardsEffect: {
      rotate: true,
      perSlideRotate: 4,
      perSlideOffset: 5,
      slideShadows: false,
    },
    pagination: {
      el: '.swiper-pagination--template--27935319916710__products_hotspot_9BRLnf',
      clickable: true,
    },
     on: {
      slideChange: function () {
        const activeIndex = this.realIndex;

        customDots.forEach((d) => d.classList.remove('active'));
        customDots[activeIndex]?.classList.add('active');
      },
    },
  });
  

  // default active
  customDots[cards_swiper.realIndex]?.classList.add('active');

  customDots.forEach((dot) => {
    dot.addEventListener('click', function () {
      const index = Number(this.dataset.index);

      cards_swiper.slideTo(index);
    });
  });
 });
</script>


</div>
```

```html
<script>
whenSwiperReady(() => {

  /* ===============================
     THUMBNAIL SWIPER 
     =============================== */
  const swiper = new Swiper(".product_thumbnail--template--27935319916710__product_slider_3T4PmL", {
    spaceBetween: 20,
    slidesPerView: 8,
    freeMode: true,
    loop: false,
    watchSlidesProgress: true,
    breakpoints: {
      320: {
        slidesPerView: 4,
        spaceBetween: 10,
      },
      640: {
        slidesPerView: 6,
        spaceBetween: 10,
      },
      1024: {
        slidesPerView: 8,
        spaceBetween: 20,
      },
    },
  });

  /* ===============================
     MAIN IMAGE SWIPER
     =============================== */
  const swiper2 = new Swiper(".product_img_container--template--27935319916710__product_slider_3T4PmL", {
    spaceBetween: 10,
    slidesPerView: 1,
    centeredSlides: true,
    loop: false,
    initialSlide: 1, // Force 2nd slide by default
    navigation: {
      nextEl: ".swiperButton_next--template--27935319916710__product_slider_3T4PmL",
      prevEl: ".swiperButton_prev--template--27935319916710__product_slider_3T4PmL",
    },
    thumbs: {
      swiper: swiper,
    },
    breakpoints: {
      769: {
        slidesPerView: 3,
        spaceBetween: 50,
      },
      1024: {
        slidesPerView: 3,
        spaceBetween: 100,
      },
    },
  });

 
  swiper2.on('init', function () {
    if (swiper2.slides.length > 1) {
      swiper2.slideTo(1, 0); // 2nd slide (index 1)
    }
  });

  // If swiper already initialized
  if (swiper2.initialized && swiper2.slides.length > 1) {
    swiper2.slideTo(1, 0);
  }

  /* ===============================
     ARROW PROXY
     =============================== */
  const swiperPrev = document.querySelector(".swiperButton_prev--template--27935319916710__product_slider_3T4PmL");
  const swiperNext = document.querySelector(".swiperButton_next--template--27935319916710__product_slider_3T4PmL");

  document.querySelector(".swiper_button_prev")?.addEventListener("click", () => {
    swiperPrev?.click();
  });

  document.querySelector(".swiper_button_next")?.addEventListener("click", () => {
    swiperNext?.click();
  });

  /* ===============================
     REMOVE THUMBNAILS FROM TAB ORDER
     =============================== */

  function disableThumbnailTabbing(swiperInstance) {
    const update = () => {
      swiperInstance.slides.forEach(slide => {
        slide.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1');
        slide.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');

        slide.querySelectorAll(
          'a, button, input, textarea, select, [tabindex]'
        ).forEach(el => {
          el.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1');
          el.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
        });
      });
    };

    swiperInstance.on('init', update);
    swiperInstance.on('slideChange', update);
    swiperInstance.on('transitionEnd', update);

    update();
  }

  disableThumbnailTabbing(swiper);

});

</script>



<style> #shopify-section-template--27935319916710__product_slider_3T4PmL {margin-top: 6px;} </style></div>
```

```html
      <p class="countdown-text" style="color:#f0e1cb;">Indulge in your glow-up essentials at half the price. Discover premium beauty and skincare products crafted to nourish, hydrate, and radiate confidence.</p>
    
    <div class="countdown-wrapper" data-end-time="2027-01-30 23:59">
      <div class="countdown-item" style="color: #331f17; background: #f0e1cb">
        <span data-days="" class="countdown-animate">296</span>
        <small>Days</small>
      </div>
      <div class="countdown-item" style="color: #331f17; background: #f0e1cb">

        <small>Hrs</small>
      </div>

        <small>Min</small>
      </div>
      <div class="countdown-item" style="color: #331f17; background: #f0e1cb">
        <span data-seconds="" class="countdown-animate">52</span>

<script>
  (function () {
    const wrapper = document.currentScript.previousElementSibling.querySelector('.countdown-wrapper');
    if (!wrapper) return;

    const endTime = new Date(wrapper.dataset.endTime).getTime();
    const d = wrapper.querySelector('[data-days]');
    const h = wrapper.querySelector('[data-hours]');
    const m = wrapper.querySelector('[data-minutes]');
    const s = wrapper.querySelector('[data-seconds]');

    function updateValue(el, value) {
      if (el.textContent !== value) {
        el.textContent = value;

        el.classList.remove('countdown-animate');
        void el.offsetWidth; //  reflow to restart animation
        el.classList.add('countdown-animate');
      }
    }

    function tick() {
      const now = new Date().getTime();
      const diff = endTime - now;

      if (diff <= 0) {
        updateValue(d, '00');
        updateValue(h, '00');
        updateValue(m, '00');
        updateValue(s, '00');
        return;
      }

      const days = String(Math.floor(diff / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24))).padStart(2, '0');

      const hours = String(Math.floor((diff / (1000 * 60 * 60)) % 24)).padStart(2, '0');

      const minutes = String(Math.floor((diff / (1000 * 60)) % 60)).padStart(2, '0');

      const seconds = String(Math.floor((diff / 1000) % 60)).padStart(2, '0');

      updateValue(d, days);
      updateValue(h, hours);
      updateValue(m, minutes);
      updateValue(s, seconds);
    }

    tick();
    setInterval(tick, 1000);
  })();
</script>

<style> #shopify-section-template--27935319916710__countdown_fQUeUQ {margin-top: 12px;} </style></div>
```

```html
  <script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
      document.querySelectorAll('.featured_blog_info').forEach((slider) => {
        const section = slider.closest('[id^="shopify-section-"]');
        if (!section) return;

        const paginationEl = section.querySelector('.mobil_swiper-pagination-featured-blog');
        const nextBtn = section.querySelector('.swiper-buttonNext');
        const prevBtn = section.querySelector('.swiper-buttonPrev');

        whenSwiperReady(() => {
          new Swiper(slider, {
            slidesPerView: 1,
            spaceBetween: 10,

            navigation: {
              nextEl: nextBtn,
              prevEl: prevBtn,
            },

            pagination: paginationEl
              ? {
                  el: paginationEl,
                  clickable: true,
                  enabled: true,
                }
              : false,

            breakpoints: {
              1024: {
                slidesPerView: 1.3,
                pagination: { enabled: true },
              },
              1440: {
                slidesPerView: 2,
                pagination: { enabled: false }, // desktop off
              },
            },
          });
        });
      });
    });
  </script>


</div>
```

```html
<script>
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    document.querySelectorAll('.image_gallery_feeds').forEach((slider) => {
      const section = slider.closest('[id^="shopify-section-"]');
      if (!section) return;

      const paginationEl = section.querySelector('.mobil_swiper-pagination-image-gallery');
      const nextBtn = section.querySelector('.gallerySwiperBtnNext');
      const prevBtn = section.querySelector('.gallerySwiperBtnPrev');

      whenSwiperReady(() => {
        new Swiper(slider, {
          slidesPerView: 1,
          spaceBetween: 10,
          autoplay: slider.dataset.autoplay === 'true',

          navigation: {
            nextEl: nextBtn,
            prevEl: prevBtn,
          },

          pagination: paginationEl
            ? {
                el: paginationEl,
                clickable: true,
                enabled: true,
              }
            : false,

          breakpoints: {
            425: {
              slidesPerView: 2,
              spaceBetween: 10,
              pagination: { enabled: true },
            },
            989: {
              slidesPerView: 2.5,
              spaceBetween: 10,
              pagination: { enabled: true },
            },
            1024: {
              slidesPerView: 3,
              spaceBetween: 20,
              pagination: { enabled: true },
            },
            1500: {
              slidesPerView: 5,
              spaceBetween: 20,
              pagination: { enabled: false },
            },
          },
        });
      });
    });
  });
</script>

</div>
```
